# 通过URL读取gzipped data

```python
#使用的还是urllib.request和zip包
import urllib.request
import gzip
# variable for URL
request_URL = 'https://web.stanford.edu/class/gene211/handouts/Homo_sapiens.GRCh38.chr21-truncated.gtf.gz'
# open stream for data
response = urllib.request.urlopen(request_URL)
# open gzipped connection
with gzip.open(response, 'rt') as inFile:
    # parse the stream line by line
    idx = 0
    for line in inFile:
        if idx < 5:
            line = line.rstrip('\n')
            print(line)
            idx =+ 1
        ### Parsing code goes here ###
```

# 从URL读取text data

```
import urllib.request
# variable for URL
request_URL = '** plain text file URL **'
# open the byte stream for data
with urllib.request.urlopen(request_URL) as inStream:
    # parse the stream line by line
    for line in inStream:
        # must decode the data into the utf-8 character set
        line = line.decode('utf-8').rstrip('\n')
        ### Parsing of file goes here ###
```
